<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(ii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company shall cooperate, and use its reasonable best efforts to cause the Company&#146;s independent certified
public accounts (the &#147;<U>Company&#146;s Auditors</U>&#148;) to cooperate, with MDLZ to the extent reasonably requested in writing by MDLZ in the preparation of the Mondel&#275;z International Public Filings. The Company agrees to use its
reasonable best efforts to provide to MDLZ all information that MDLZ reasonably requests in writing in connection with any Mondel&#275;z International Public Filings that, in the reasonable judgment of MDLZ upon consultation with its legal counsel,
is required to be disclosed or incorporated by reference therein under any applicable Law. The Company shall use its reasonable best efforts to provide such information to enable Mondel&#275;z International to prepare and release all Mondel&#275;z
International Public Filings on a timely basis. To the extent required in such filing, the Company shall use its reasonable best efforts to cause the Company&#146;s Auditors to consent to any reference to them as experts in any Mondel&#275;z
International Public Filings required under applicable Law; </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iii)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company and MDLZ shall share with each other
(subject to any agreed protocols) aggregate security position information, within 60 days after the end of each fiscal quarter, for use in their respective compliance programs and shall coordinate share ownership reporting for such purpose; and </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(iv)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company will, within 25 days after the end of each fiscal quarter, make the Company&#146;s controller available
for a discussion with MDLZ with regards to updates to the Company&#146;s business and financial results with respect to such fiscal quarter. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;With respect to any information provided by the Company: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:8%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(i)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Subject to the requirements of law and to except the extent required to be included in Mondel&#275;z International

<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>HOLDERS OF REGISTRABLE SECURITIES </U></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Maple

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>ANNEX A </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><U>FORM OF SELLING SECURITYHOLDER NOTICE, AGREEMENT AND QUESTIONNAIRE </U></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The undersigned (the &#147;<U>Selling Securityholder</U>&#148;) beneficial owner of common stock, par value $0.01 (the &#147;<U>Common
Stock</U>&#148;), of Keurig Dr Pepper Inc. (the &#147;<U>Company</U>&#148;) understands that the Company intends to file with the Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#147;<U>SEC</U>&#148;) a registration statement on Form <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">S-3</FONT> or a prospectus supplement to an existing shelf registration statement (as applicable, the &#147;<U>Shelf Registration Statement</U>&#148;) for the registration and resale under Rule 415 of the Securities Act of
1933, as amended (the &#147;<U>Securities Act</U>&#148;), of certain Registrable Securities in accordance with the terms of the Investor Rights Agreement, dated on or about July&nbsp;9, 2018 (the &#147;<U>Investor Rights Agreement</U>&#148;), by and
among the Company and the persons listed on <U>Schedule A</U> hereto. Each capitalized term not otherwise defined herein has the meaning given to it in the Investor Rights Agreement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In order to sell or otherwise dispose of any Registrable Securities pursuant to the Shelf Registration Statement, the Selling Securityholder
must be named as a selling securityholder in the related prospectus and deliver a prospectus to the purchasers of Registrable Securities. To facilitate naming of the Selling Securityholder as a selling securityholder in the Shelf Registration
Statement, the Selling Securityholder must complete, execute, acknowledge and deliver this Notice, Agreement and Questionnaire prior to filing of the prospectus supplement to the Shelf Registration Statement. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain legal consequences arise from being named as Selling Securityholders in the Shelf Registration Statement and the related prospectus.
Accordingly, the Selling Securityholder is advised to consult its own legal counsel regarding the consequences of being named or not being named as a Selling Securityholder in the Shelf Registration Statement and the related prospectus. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Selling Securityholder hereby gives notice to the Company of its intention to sell or otherwise dispose of
Registrable Securities beneficially owned by it and listed below in Item 3(b) pursuant to the Shelf Registration Statement. The Selling Securityholder, by signing and returning this Notice, Agreement and Questionnaire, understands that it shall be
bound by the terms and conditions of this Notice, Agreement and Questionnaire. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;The Selling Securityholder
hereby provides the following information to the Company and represents and warrants that such information is accurate and complete: </P>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Appendix A </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>DEFINITION OF &#147;BENEFICIAL OWNERSHIP&#148; </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A &#147;Beneficial Owner&#148; of a security includes any person who, directly or indirectly, through any contract, arrangement, understanding, relationship or otherwise has or shares: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(a) Voting power which includes the power to vote, or to direct the voting of, such security; and/or </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(b) Investment power which includes the power to dispose, or direct the disposition of, such security. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Please note that either voting power or investment power, or both, is sufficient for you to be considered the beneficial owner of shares. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Any person who, directly or indirectly, creates or uses a trust, proxy, power of attorney, pooling arrangement or any other contract, arrangement or device with the purpose or effect of divesting such person of
beneficial ownership of a security or preventing the vesting of such beneficial ownership as part of a plan or scheme to evade the reporting requirements of the federal securities acts shall be deemed to be the beneficial owner of such security.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="4%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Notwithstanding the provisions of paragraph (1), a person is deemed to be the &#147;beneficial owner&#148; of a security if that person has the right to acquire beneficial ownership of such security within 60 days,
including but not limited to any right to acquire: (a)&nbsp;through the exercise of any option, warrant or right; (b)&nbsp;through the conversion of a security; (c)&nbsp;pursuant to the power to revoke a trust, discretionary account or similar
arrangement; or (d)&nbsp;pursuant to the automatic termination of a trust, discretionary account or similar arrangement; <U>provided</U>, <U>however</U>, any person who acquires a security or power specified in (a), (b) or (c)&nbsp;above, with the
purpose or effect of changing or influencing the control of the issuer, or in connection with or as a participant in any transaction having such purpose or effect, immediately upon such acquisition shall be deemed to be the beneficial owner of the
securities which may be acquired through the exercise or conversion of such security or power. </TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD VALIGN="bottom"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:1.00em; text-indent:-1.00em; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">1. Interpretation</P></TD>

<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the development, manufacturing, marketing and sales of: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

provide for the preparation of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-demand</FONT> Coffee and Coffee Beverages or Tea and Tea Beverages or Chocolate Beverages; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

and/or dominant ingredient and/or flavour component, either carbonated or <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-carbonated,</FONT> </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:23%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">in all distribution channels, including retail/fast moving consumer goods, wholesale, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-</FONT> <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">of-</FONT> home, coffee shops, instant consumption, modern trade, traditional trade, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> and whether distributed directly or indirectly through distributors or wholesalers;

or juice concentrates whether or not sold simultaneously with coffee) offered in conjunction with Coffee Beverages as an ancillary offering to the main coffee portfolio, in each case only intended for use in out of home coffee machines and
(y)&nbsp;other non coffee products which complement the coffee out of home coffee portfolio (sugar, milk and chocolate powder in single portioned sticks/containers, single wrapped cookies, single wrapped chocolate and stir sticks) as an ancillary
offering to Coffee Beverages dispensed through coffee machines (which include machines that dispense other beverages as long as coffee is in the main offering) in the out of home distribution channel only. For the avoidance of doubt, it is not
intended that chocolate, Chocolate Beverages or such other non coffee products will form part of the Business other than in the limited circumstances set out in paragraph (b)(iii) and this paragraph (c); and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the marketing and sales of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-demand</FONT> brewing systems for Coffee Beverages and Tea Beverages including brewers and accessories through direct consumer, online or <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">out-of-home</FONT></FONT> distribution channels and the development and/or manufacturing of the same through third party cooperation. </TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.2.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to clause 3.2.7, the Shareholders shall appoint both the CEO and CFO (but not only one of them) to act as the Management Directors. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.2.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Management Directors shall be tax residents of the Netherlands and a majority of the Directors shall not be resident in the same jurisdiction unless that jurisdiction is the Netherlands or the United States of
America. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.2.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Directors at Closing shall be as set out in schedule 3. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.2.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">With effect from Closing, until the earlier of (i)&nbsp;Anna-Lena Kamenetzky ceasing to be a Director and (ii)&nbsp;the appointment of a new CFO (the &#147;<B>Term</B>&#148;), Anna-Lena Kamenetzky shall serve as a non
executive Director (but not, for the avoidance of doubt an A Director or a Management Director) in place of the CFO named in Schedule 5. At the end of the Term, the B Shareholder shall be entitled to require that the CFO named in Schedule 5 or the
new CFO (as the case may be) be appointed to act as a Management Director. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;6&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Appointment and removal of Directors</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Any appointment or removal of an A Director or a B Director by the A Shareholder or the B Shareholder (as the case may be) shall be made by such Shareholder giving written notice to the Company (with a copy to the other
Shareholder). The appointment or removal shall, to the extent permitted by Law, take effect immediately upon receipt of the notice by the Company or such later date specified by the Shareholder in the notice. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If an A Director or a B Director dies, resigns, is removed or retires, the A Shareholder or the B Shareholder (as the case may be) may appoint another Director in accordance with this clause 3. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If at any time the A Shareholder or the B Shareholder ceases to own a single Share or if there is a Step Down in relation to the B Shareholder, the A Shareholder or the B Shareholder (as the case may be) shall promptly
procure the resignation of each Director appointed by it or, if there is a Step Down, the relevant number of Directors appointed by it. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Any Shareholder who removes a Director appointed by it in accordance with the terms of this Agreement shall indemnify and keep indemnified the other Shareholder and any Group Company on demand against all losses,
liabilities and costs which such person may incur arising out of, or in connection with, any claim by such Director for wrongful or unfair dismissal, redundancy or otherwise arising out of such Director&#146;s ceasing to hold office.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Shareholders (following the recommendation of the Board) may remove a Management Director at any time and must remove a Management Director if he ceases to be CEO or CFO (as the case may be). No Management Director
may vote on his own appointment or removal. If the CEO or CFO is removed from the Board, the Shareholders (following the recommendation of the Board) shall appoint his successor (nominated in accordance with clause 5.1.2) to the Board.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Chairman</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.4.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The A Shareholder shall be entitled to appoint and remove any A Director as the Chairman of the Board (the &#147;<B>Chairman</B>&#148;) by giving written notice to the Company (with a copy to the B Shareholder).
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.4.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Chairman at Closing shall be as set out in schedule 3. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.4.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Chairman shall preside at any Board meeting at which he is present and shall be responsible for administering the work of the Board so as to ensure good order without favouring any of the Directors or Shareholders
or any particular proposal and to afford all Directors an opportunity to participate fully. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;7&nbsp;- </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.4.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the Chairman for the time being is unable to attend any Board meeting, a majority of the A Directors attending such meeting shall be entitled to appoint one of their number to act as chairman at such meeting only.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Subsidiary boards</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Unless required by local Law or regulation or the terms of any
collective bargaining agreement, the directors of the boards of all other Group Companies shall comprise Directors, members of the Executive Team or employees of the Group, in each case who are suitably qualified and competent for the position. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Committees</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to applicable Law, Directors may delegate any of their powers to a committee of the Board constituted under this clause 3.6, save for the power to resolve on a Reserved Matter or a Board Authority Matter.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to clause 3.6.4, the Board shall determine the composition of any such committee as they see fit, save that:<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top"> </SUP> </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the A Shareholder shall be entitled to appoint at least one Director to each such committee, and to remove any such appointment from time to time, by giving written notice to the Company (with a copy to the B
Shareholder); and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the B Shareholder shall be entitled to appoint at least one Director to each such committee, and to remove any such appointment from time to time, by giving written notice to the Company (with a copy to the A
Shareholder). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The voting and quorum requirements for meetings of any such committees shall be the same as for Board meetings. Each committee member will have one vote each. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Audit Committee and Compensation Committee shall be comprised of Directors. The initial composition of the committees at Closing shall be as set out in parts A and B respectively of schedule 4. The Shareholders
intend no change to the composition of these committees for the first 12 months following Closing. The Audit Committee and Compensation Committee shall have the terms of reference set out in parts A and B respectively of schedule 4.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The A Shareholder shall be entitled to appoint and remove any Director as the chairman of the Compensation Committee by giving written notice to the Company (with a copy to the B Shareholder). </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The B Shareholder shall be entitled to appoint and remove any Director as the chairman of the Audit Committee by giving written notice to the Company (with a copy to the A shareholder). </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;8&nbsp;- </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Remuneration and expenses of Directors</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Directors shall be entitled to receive
repayment of reasonable expenses incurred in relation to the performance of their duties as Directors and, if so determined by the Board, to reasonable fees for acting in their capacity as such and for sitting on committees in equal amounts (except
that the Chairman and the chairman of the Audit Committee and the Compensation Committee may receive a higher amount for serving as such). For the avoidance of doubt, the Board can only decide to pay director&#146;s fees to all Directors or to no
Directors. Directors shall not otherwise be entitled to receive any remuneration by way of salary, commission, fees or otherwise in relation to the performance of their duties as Directors. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Directors&#146; insurance and indemnity</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.8.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Company shall maintain adequate directors&#146; and officers&#146; liability insurance for the benefit of the Directors. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.8.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Company shall provide the Directors with the benefit of an indemnity against any liability which the Directors may incur in relation to the Group to the extent permitted by applicable Law. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Secretary</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board may, in its discretion, appoint an individual to act as secretary
to the Board to assist the Chairman and the Board with such administrative matters as the Chairman or the Board, as applicable, deem appropriate. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>PROCEEDINGS OF DIRECTORS</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Convening Board meetings</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Directors shall hold Board meetings at least four times in each Financial Year and at least once every fiscal quarter (&#147;<B>Quarterly Meetings</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">At any time any Director may request the Chairman to convene a Board meeting and such meeting shall be convened in accordance with clauses 4.2.2 and 4.2.3 as soon as practicable following receipt of such request.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.1.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Board meetings will be held in locations so that the effective place of management of the Company is the Netherlands and to avoid the risk of the Company being treated as a taxable resident of any other jurisdiction or
creating a taxable presence of the Company in any other jurisdiction. In particular, the parties will comply with the terms of any relevant Dutch ruling addressing the effective place of management of the Company. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Notice </B><B>of Board meetings</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.2.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The dates for Quarterly Meetings shall be fixed and communicated to the Directors as early as possible, but not later than 9 months in advance. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.2.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">At least 10 Business Days&#146; written notice shall be given to each Director of other Board meetings unless
(a)&nbsp;clause 4.3.2 applies, (b)&nbsp;each of the Directors </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL
TREATMENT HAS BEEN REQUESTED FOR PORTIONS OF THIS EXHIBIT. THE COPY FILED HEREWITH OMITS THE INFORMATION SUBJECT TO A CONFIDENTIALITY REQUEST. OMISSIONS ARE DESIGNATED [&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;]. A COMPLETE VERSION OF THIS EXHIBIT HAS BEEN FILED
SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;9&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
approves a shorter notice period, or (c)&nbsp;the Chairman determines, acting reasonably, that there is a significant and time sensitive matter that requires shorter notice to be given, in which
case the Chairman may convene a meeting (a &#147;<B>Short Notice Meeting</B>&#148;) by giving at least 24 hours&#146; written notice to each other Director. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.2.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">An agenda identifying in reasonable detail the matters to be discussed at a Board meeting together with copies of any relevant papers to be discussed at the meeting shall be provided to each Director, if practicable, at
the same time as notice is given of such meeting and otherwise at least 7 days prior to the date on which the meeting is to be held. In the case of a Short Notice Meeting, the notice convening the meeting shall set out in as much detail as possible
the reasons for the meeting. If any matter is not identified in reasonable detail, the Directors shall not decide on it, unless all the Directors agree. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.2.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Notice of meetings, the agenda and copies of any relevant papers may be delivered to the Directors by email, unless and until any Director instructs the Company otherwise with respect to delivery to him.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Quorum at Board meetings</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">No business shall be transacted at any meeting of the Board unless a quorum is present at the time when the meeting proceeds to business and remains present during the transaction of such business. Subject to clause
4.4, the quorum for transacting business at any Board meeting shall be at least one A Director and at least one B Director. A Director shall be regarded as present for the purposes of a quorum if represented by an attorney appointed in accordance
with clause 4.6. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If a quorum is not present at a duly convened Board meeting, the meeting shall be adjourned to another date by notice given in accordance with clause 4.2, except that in this case, only 5 Business Days&#146; notice of
the adjourned meeting needs to be given. The quorum at such adjourned meeting shall be as set out in clause 4.3.1. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Voting at Board meetings</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On any vote on a resolution of the Directors, each Director
shall have one vote. Subject to the specific requirements in clause 6 relating to Reserved Matters (a)&nbsp;resolutions of the Directors shall be decided by simple majority vote and (b)&nbsp;if a vote of the Directors is tied, the Chairman (or the
Director acting as chairman at the relevant meeting in accordance with clause 3.4.4) will have a casting vote. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Conflict</B><B> of interest</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.5.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">In respect of any right of action by the Company or any other Group Company against the Shareholder who appointed him or any of its Affiliates or any right of action by the Shareholder who appointed him or any of its
Affiliates against the Company or any other Group Company, a Director shall not be entitled to receive board papers, attend or be counted in the quorum or vote at a Board meeting on any resolution in respect of any such matters unless otherwise
agreed in writing by the Shareholder that did not appoint him. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;10&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.5.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A Management Director shall not be entitled to vote at a Board meeting on any resolution relating to (a)&nbsp;his appointment or removal from the Board or (b)&nbsp;his own remuneration. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Power of attorney</B><B> </B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Any Director shall be entitled to authorise any other
Director, at any time, to act on his behalf by the appointment of such other Director as his attorney under a specific power of attorney. Any such appointment shall be confirmed in writing (which can be by email) to the Company. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Participation in Board meetings</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The intention is that Quarterly Meetings will be held
in person and other Board meetings will be held in person wherever this is practicable. That said, a Director (or his attorney) may participate in a Board meeting by means of a conference telephone or similar form of communications equipment which
allows all persons participating in the meeting to hear and speak to each other throughout the meeting. A person participating in this way is deemed to be present in person at the meeting and is counted in the quorum and entitled to vote. Taking
into consideration clause 4.1.3, if all the Directors participating in the meeting are not in the same place, they may decide that the meeting is to be treated as taking place wherever any of them is (but in no event shall a Board meeting be treated
as taking place in the United States of America). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Written resolution of Directors</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.8.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">At least 5 Business Days&#146; written notice of a proposed Directors&#146; written resolution without a meeting of the Board shall be given to each Director, unless each of the Directors approves a shorter notice
period. Such notice shall be accompanied by relevant papers no less detailed than those which would be provided in advance of a Board meeting in accordance with clause 4.2. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.8.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A Directors&#146; written resolution is adopted when the requisite voting majority of Directors (determined in accordance with clause 4.4) have signed one or more copies of it. A written resolution signed by an attorney
appointed in accordance with clause 4.6 need not also be signed by his appointor and, if it is signed by his appointor, it need not be signed by the attorney in that capacity. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.8.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Once a Directors&#146; written resolution has been adopted, it shall be treated as if it had been a decision taken at a Board meeting in accordance with this Agreement. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>No breach of duty</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A Director shall not be in breach of his duties to the Company by
reason of his acting in accordance with this clause&nbsp;4.9 or otherwise in accordance with the terms of this Agreement and the Articles. Accordingly, each Shareholder authorises each Director: </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;11&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.9.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to act as a Director notwithstanding his appointment by a Shareholder for the purposes of representing such Shareholder&#146;s interests and monitoring and evaluating its investment in the Company and the Group;
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.9.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to receive and deal with Confidential Information and other documents and information relating to any Group Company or its business or assets and to use and apply such information in representing the interests of the
Shareholder that appointed him; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.9.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to disclose any Confidential Information to any director, officer or employee of any Shareholder that appointed him or any director, officer or employee of its Shareholder Group Entities to the extent necessary for the
purposes of monitoring and evaluating such Shareholder&#146;s participation in the Company and the Group; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.9.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to keep confidential any information relating to the Shareholder that appointed him or any of its Affiliates that is subject to obligations of confidence and which such Shareholder is not otherwise obliged to disclose
to the other Shareholder or any Group Company pursuant to the terms of this Agreement and not to use or apply such information in performing his duties to the Company or any Group Company. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>THE EXECUTIVE TEAM</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Appointment of the Executive Team </B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">It is intended that the Executive Team at Closing shall be as set out in schedule 5. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The appointment or removal of the Executive Team after Closing shall be determined by the Board, in accordance with the following: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in relation to the appointment of a new CEO in his capacity as an officer of the Company, the A Shareholder shall have the right to submit to the Board a shortlist of suitably qualified and competent candidates for the
appointment of the CEO, and the Board will appoint a CEO from that list. If the Board cannot resolve upon an appointment from the shortlist, the A Shareholder shall submit revised shortlists from which the CEO shall be appointed; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in relation to the appointment of a new CFO in his capacity as an officer of the Company, the B Shareholder shall have the right to submit to the Board a shortlist of suitably qualified and competent candidates for the
appointment of the CFO, and the Board will appoint a CFO from that list. If the Board cannot resolve upon an appointment from the shortlist, the B Shareholder shall submit revised shortlists from which the CFO shall be appointed; and
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in relation to the appointment of any other member of the Executive Team, the Board will cooperate to create a shortlist of candidates taking into account recommendations from both the A and B Shareholders, and the
Board will appoint a candidate from that list. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Responsibilities of the Executive Team</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Subject to the Reserved Matters and the Board
Authority Matters, the Board may delegate to the Executive Team the power to manage and administer the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">day-to-day</FONT></FONT> activities of the Group in accordance with the
Strategic Plan, the Annual Contract, the Articles and this Agreement under the overall direction and supervision of the Board. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Remuneration of the Executive Team</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Board shall agree on a remuneration policy for
the Executive Team having regard to the recommendations of the Compensation Committee. The Executive Team and other senior employees of the Group shall be incentivised (among other things) on the basis of the Group&#146;s performance against the
Annual Contract and, save for any Existing External Benefits, shall not receive any remuneration or benefit of whatever nature from any of the Shareholders or their respective Affiliates without the prior consent of the Board. The Management
Directors shall not be entitled to vote on their own remuneration. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Oversight of Governance Policies</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.4.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Board shall cause the CFO to submit to the Board a shortlist of suitably qualified and competent candidates for the appointment of a person who is knowledgeable regarding the implementation and operation of the
Governance Policies (the &#147;<B>Compliance Officer</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">5.4.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Compliance Officer shall have the duties and responsibilities set out in part C of schedule 4. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>RESERVED MATTERS </B><B>AND BOARD AUTHORITY MATTERS</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Company shall not take, and shall procure that no other Group Company takes, any action in respect of any Reserved Matter without either: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the prior approval of the Board given by way of a Board resolution adopted at a validly convened Board meeting, with a majority of the A Directors and a majority of the B Directors voting in favour; or
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the prior written approval of a majority of the A Directors and a majority of the B Directors, given by way of a Board written resolution adopted in accordance with clause 4.8. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Each Reserved Matter shall be considered and, if thought fit, approved independently of each other Reserved Matter. Approval of a Reserved Matter constituted by a proposal shall not constitute approval of another
Reserved Matter constituted by the same proposal. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">If a Reserved Matter or other action approved by the Board in accordance with this Agreement also requires the
approval of Shareholders under applicable Law, the Company and the Shareholders shall procure that a Shareholder meeting is convened </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL
TREATMENT HAS BEEN REQUESTED FOR PORTIONS OF THIS EXHIBIT. THE COPY FILED HEREWITH OMITS THE INFORMATION SUBJECT TO A CONFIDENTIALITY REQUEST. OMISSIONS ARE DESIGNATED [&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;]. A COMPLETE VERSION OF THIS EXHIBIT HAS BEEN FILED
SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>
