<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
or a Shareholders&#146; written resolution is passed as soon as reasonably practical following approval of the Reserved Matter by the Board in accordance with clause 6.1 and each Shareholder
undertakes to use its voting rights to give effect to the Reserved Matter so approved. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Schedule 2 contains a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-exhaustive</FONT> list of actions by a Group Company which must be considered by the Board of the Company at a duly convened Board meeting (&#147;<B>Board
Authority Matters</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">6.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">In determining whether a matter is a Reserved Matter or a Board Authority Matter, a series of related transactions shall be construed as a single transaction, and any amounts involved in the related transactions shall
be aggregated. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>DEADLOCK</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Deadlock</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A deadlock (a &#147;<B>Deadlock</B>&#148;) shall have occurred if a bona fide proposal in respect of any Reserved Matter has not been approved in accordance with clause 6.1 and the A Shareholder or the B Shareholder (as
the case may be) notifies the other in writing that it regards such proposal (the &#147;<B>Deadlock Matter</B>&#148;)<B> </B>as not having been agreed and that a Deadlock has arisen (a &#147;<B>Deadlock Notice</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">While a Deadlock exists, each Shareholder shall exercise all such rights and powers as are available to it to enable the Group to continue operating in the ordinary course of its business and in accordance with the
terms of this Agreement, provided that no action shall be taken in relation to the matter which is the subject of the Deadlock, save as contemplated by clause 7.2. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Escalation</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.2.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Following the giving of a Deadlock Notice, the A and B Shareholders shall immediately refer the Deadlock Matter to: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in the case of the A Shareholder, the chairman, senior partner or chief executive officer of the JAB Holding Company Group as notified by the A Shareholder to the B Shareholder from time to time. At Closing, the A
Shareholder Escalation Representative shall be Olivier Goudet; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in the case of the B Shareholder, the chief executive officer of Mondel&#275;z International, Inc. from time to time, </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(together, the &#147;<B>Escalation Representatives</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.2.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Escalation Representatives shall, for a period of 20 Business Days starting on the Business Day after the date on which the Deadlock Notice was given (the &#147;<B>Deadlock Resolution Period</B>&#148;), attempt in
good faith to resolve the Deadlock. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL
TREATMENT HAS BEEN REQUESTED FOR PORTIONS OF THIS EXHIBIT. THE COPY FILED HEREWITH OMITS THE INFORMATION SUBJECT TO A CONFIDENTIALITY REQUEST. OMISSIONS ARE DESIGNATED [&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;]. A COMPLETE VERSION OF THIS EXHIBIT HAS BEEN FILED
SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;14&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.2.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the Escalation Representatives resolve the Deadlock Matter within the Deadlock Resolution Period, the Shareholders shall procure (in so far as they are able) that the Company acts and, if relevant, the Company shall
procure that any other Group Company acts, in accordance with the instructions given by the Escalation Representatives. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">7.2.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to clause 16.7.6, if the Escalation Representatives fail to resolve the Deadlock Matter within the Deadlock Resolution Period, the Company shall not take any action relating to the Deadlock Matter and this
Agreement shall continue to apply in accordance with its terms. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">8.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>SHAREHOLDER MEETINGS</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">All Shareholder meetings shall take place in accordance with
applicable Law and the Articles. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>STRATEGIC PLAN </B><B>AND ANNUAL CONTRACT</B><B> </B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Schedule 11 contains (a)&nbsp;the contents requirements for the Strategic Plan and the Annual Contract and (b)&nbsp;the schedule for delivery of drafts and approval by the Board. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">9.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Management Directors shall provide an update of the Group&#146;s performance against the Annual Contract at each Quarterly Meeting. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>ACCOUNTING AND REPORTING</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Accounting principles</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company shall prepare its financial statements (including its
consolidated financial statements) and management accounts in accordance with IFRS and shall procure that the financial statements are reviewed and audited in accordance with IFRS. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Reporting to the Shareholders</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to any information and reporting rights in
the Tax Matters Agreement, the Company shall supply the Shareholders with the items listed in part A of schedule 6 in accordance with the deadlines set out therein and, on a timely basis, such other information as MDLZ may reasonably require in
order to comply with the public disclosures described in part B of that schedule or to meet its or its Affiliates&#146; respective audit requirements. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Access to information</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Each Shareholder and its authorised representatives shall be allowed access at all reasonable times to examine (and at its expense to take copies of) the books and records of the Group and to discuss the Business and
affairs of the Group with the Executive Team and other relevant employees of the Group. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">10.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Each Shareholder reserves the right to undertake an audit of any Group Company (including to investigate compliance with Anti-Bribery Laws and Sanctions Laws) at its own cost, either by its own internal audit staff or
by external advisers. Such Shareholder shall give the Company at least 10 Business Days&#146; written notice of its intention to carry out such an audit. The Company shall procure that each Group Company
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-operates</FONT> with any audit required by a Shareholder pursuant to this clause 10.3.2. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

in addition to that set out in the Global Contribution Agreement, or to provide any undertaking, covenant, guarantee or performance bond or any other recourse to a Shareholder, in respect of or pursuant to any financing arrangement of the Group.

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to the requirements of applicable Law and any restrictions contained in definitive credit documents entered into in connection with the Closing Debt Documents and any other financing or refinancing permitted
hereunder, the Company shall distribute to the Shareholders no later than six months after the end of each Financial Year following Closing at least: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">12.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">&#128;175&nbsp;million with respect to the Financial Year ending 31&nbsp;December, 2016; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>

relating to such Financial Year, the Company is able to declare and pay a dividend of &#128;225&nbsp;million or more without such declaration and payment resulting in a default or event of default under, or other
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-compliance</FONT> with covenants contained in, the agreements governing the indebtedness of the Group at such time, the obligation will be to pay at least &#128;225&nbsp;million with respect to such Financial
Year; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

&#147;<B>Dividend Policy</B>&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">13.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>OTHER POLIC</B><B>IES</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Group will be managed in a way that is consistent in all
material respects with the Governance Policies. The amendment of any Governance Policy is a Reserved Matter. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>COVENANTS </B><B>-</B><B> <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-COMPETE</FONT> AND <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">NON-SOLICITATION</FONT></B> </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to clause 14.3, each Shareholder shall not (and shall procure that its Affiliates shall not), without the prior written consent of the A and B Shareholders, either alone or jointly with, through or as adviser
to, or agent of, or manager for, any person, directly or indirectly: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">carry on or be engaged, concerned or interested in or assist a business which competes, directly or indirectly, with the Business as carried on at any time during the term of this Agreement (unless otherwise agreed by
the Shareholders); </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">do or say anything which is harmful to the goodwill or reputation of the Business or any Group Company or which could reasonably lead a person who is dealing or has at any time during the term of this Agreement dealt
with the Business or any Group Company to cease to deal with the Business or any Group Company on substantially equivalent terms to those previously offered or at all. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The restrictions contained in clause 14.1 shall apply to a Shareholder and its Affiliates until the end of the period of&nbsp;two&nbsp;years from the date on which such Shareholder ceases to be a party to this
Agreement. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Nothing contained in clause 14.1 shall preclude or restrict a Shareholder or any of its Affiliates from: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">subject to clause 14.4, acquiring control of a company or business which has as an incidental part of its activities an activity which would be prohibited by this clause (a &#147;<B>Competing Business
Portion</B>&#148;); </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">holding not more than 5% of the issued share capital of any company which competes with the Business whose shares are listed on a recognised stock exchange; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.3.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">offering any service or goods similar to those previously supplied as part of the Business but subsequently discontinued and not supplied by any Group Company at the time when the similar service or goods are offered;
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.3.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">continuing to carry on or be engaged, concerned or interested in any business or person that, prior to a change in the scope of the Business agreed in accordance with this Agreement, did not compete with the Business,
but thereafter competes with the Business as a result of such modification; </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Acquisitions of a Competing Business Portion</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If a Shareholder or any of its Affiliates
(the &#147;Acquiring Shareholder&#148;) acquires control of a company or business with a Competing Business Portion, it shall offer to sell the Competing Business Portion to the Company at fair market value. If the Board, excluding for the purposes
of voting only any Directors appointed by the Acquiring Shareholder, chooses not to buy the Competing Business Portion, the Acquiring Shareholder shall as soon as reasonably practicable sell, or procure that its Affiliate sells, it to a third party
except to the extent that the Competing Business Portion operates in the United States, Canada or Mexico. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Other Interests</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.5.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Shareholders acknowledge that each of them or their Affiliates own businesses outside of their investment in the Group (each, a &#147;<B>Non JV Business</B>&#148;) and each Shareholder undertakes, either directly or
indirectly, not to share any commercially sensitive information in relation to any Non JV Business with the other or a Group Company and not to share any commercially sensitive information relating to any Group Company with any Non JV Business. In
the event that this Agreement is <U>amended</U> to <U>permit</U> a Shareholder to compete with the Business as an exception to the prohibitions in clause 14.1, the Shareholders and the Company acknowledge and agree that this Agreement will need to
be further amended to ensure that adequate antitrust compliance and information sharing procedures are put in place. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.5.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Nothing in clause 14.1 shall preclude Olivier Goudet, one of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-executive</FONT> Board members appointed by Oak and Oak Minority, from holding a
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-executive</FONT> board position at Mars Incorporated. However, Oak undertakes that it has obtained written confirmation from Olivier Goudet that he shall not (a)&nbsp;share any commercially sensitive information
in relation to the Business in connection with the performance of his/her duties as a member of the board of Mars Incorporated; and (b)&nbsp;share any commercially sensitive information in relation to the coffee or tea business of Mars Incorporated
in connection with the performance of his duties as a member of the Board. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>New Opportunity</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.6.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If a Shareholder identifies or becomes aware of any opportunity relevant to the Business in the territory referred to in clause 2.1.2 which is not expressly carved out by clause 14.3 (the &#147;<B>New
Opportunity</B>&#148;), then (unless it considers that the New Opportunity does not merit consideration by the Company) the relevant Shareholder (the &#147;<B>Referring Shareholder</B>&#148;) shall notify the Board in writing with reasonable details
as to the nature of the New Opportunity as soon as reasonably practicable and, in any event, before any material negotiations commence with any third party. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.6.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the Board, excluding for the purposes of voting only any Directors appointed by the Referring Shareholder, chooses to pursue the New Opportunity (subject always to the requisite approval if the New Opportunity is a
Reserved Matter), the Shareholders shall procure that the Group uses all reasonable endeavours to implement the New Opportunity as soon as reasonably practicable. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.6.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If (i)&nbsp;a Shareholder considers that a New Opportunity (for the avoidance of doubt, which does not include any opportunity being considered by KDP) does not merit consideration by the Company or (ii)&nbsp;the Board
(a)&nbsp;chooses to pursue the New Opportunity, but does not enter into a transaction within six months or (b)&nbsp;chooses not to pursue the New Opportunity, then neither Shareholder, nor any Affiliate, shall be entitled to proceed on its own with
such New Opportunity, except to the extent that the New Opportunity relates to the United States, Canada or Mexico. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-solicitation</FONT></B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">14.7.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Each Shareholder undertakes to the other and to the Company that for a period of 2 years from Closing it shall not (and shall procure that its Affiliates shall not), without the prior written consent of the other
Shareholder, directly or indirectly engage or employ, or solicit or contact with a view to his engagement or employment by another person, a person who is or has at any time during the term of this Agreement or in the 6 months prior to the date of
Closing been a director, officer, employee or manager of the Business or any Group Company where the person in question either has Confidential Information or knowhow or would be in a position to exploit the Business&#146; or Group&#146;s trade
connections. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

Shareholder may transfer its Shares: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Transfers to Shareholder Group Entities</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A Shareholder may transfer all (but not only some) of its Shares to a Shareholder Group Entity at any time on giving prior written notice to the other Shareholders, copied to the Company, provided that:
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in the case of the A Shareholder, such transfer would not cause a deemed termination and reformation of a partnership for US tax purposes, unless: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="23%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(i)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the A Shareholder has consulted with the B Shareholder and the B Shareholder has determined in its reasonable judgement that the transfer would not have a material adverse impact on the B Shareholder; or
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="23%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(ii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the A Shareholder indemnifies the B Shareholder for any US tax paid as a result of such termination and reformation; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the transferee shall first have entered into a Deed of Adherence in the form set out in schedule 8; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the transferee ceases to be a Shareholder Group Entity, the transferee shall prior to such cessation transfer all the Shares held by it to the transferring Shareholder or to another Shareholder Group Entity in
accordance with and as permitted by this Agreement; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the transferring Shareholder shall procure that the Shareholder Group Entity to whom Shares are transferred in accordance with this clause 15.3.1 complies with the terms of this Agreement. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(e)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Following a transfer to a Shareholder Group Entity in accordance with this clause 15.3 any references in this Agreement to Shares held by a Shareholder shall be deemed to be a reference to Shares held by the Shareholder
Group Entity to whom it has transferred Shares in accordance with this clause 15.3. </TD></TR></TABLE>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Notwithstanding anything contained herein to the contrary, each of Oak and Oak Minority may transfer all of its Shares to the other, subject to compliance with clasue 15.3.1. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Transfers after third anniversary of Closing</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.4.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">After 2&nbsp;July 2018: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the B Shareholder may invoke the provisions of clause 15.5 (a &#147;<B>ROFO Process</B>&#148;); </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the A Shareholder may invoke the provisions of clause 15.6 (an &#147;<B>IPO Process</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.4.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The B Shareholder may also invoke an IPO Process in the circumstances set out in clause 15.5.5. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.4.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Once a Shareholder has initiated a ROFO Process or an IPO Process (an &#147;<B>Initial Process</B>&#148;), the other Shareholder may not serve a competing notice or a Default Notice: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the Initial Process is a ROFO Process, before the date which is 15 Business Days after the first to occur of (i)&nbsp;expiry of the Offer Period (if no Offer is made) and (ii)&nbsp;the date on which a Response Notice
is given (or deemed to be given) which constitutes a rejection of an Offer; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the Initial Process is an IPO Process, before the date which is 15 Business Days (if the competing notice is a Default Notice) or 3 months (if the competing notice is a ROFO Notice or an IPO Notice) after the first
to occur of (i)&nbsp;expiry of the Consideration Period if no IPO Acceptance Notice is given and (ii)&nbsp;the date of a Termination Notice. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.4.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">For the avoidance of doubt, any IPO Process is with respect to a listing of a Shareholder&#146;s Shares only. Any issuance of new Shares in connection with an IPO shall be a Reserved Matter. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.4.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Following an Initial IPO, the provisions of clauses 15.1 to 15.6 shall no longer apply and clause 15.7 shall apply. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Right of First </B><B>Offer</B><B> Process</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to clause 15.4, if the B Shareholder wishes to transfer its Shares (the &#147;<B>Sale Shares</B>&#148;) it shall serve a written notice (a &#147;<B>ROFO Notice</B>&#148;) on the A Shareholder. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Within [ * * * ] Business Days of the date of the ROFO Notice (the &#147;<B>Offer Period</B>&#148;), the A Shareholder may by notice in writing to the B Shareholder (an &#147;<B>Offer</B>&#148;) make a bona fide offer
to acquire all of the Sale Shares. The Offer must set out the price per Sale Share (the &#147;<B>Offer Price</B>&#148;) and any other terms on which the A Shareholder offers to acquire the Sale Shares. Once made, an Offer shall be irrevocable and
binding and shall be accepted or rejected by the B Shareholder in accordance with clause 15.5.3. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Within [ * * * ] Business Days of the date of the Offer (the &#147;<B>Acceptance Period</B>&#148;), the B Shareholder must inform the A Shareholder in writing (a &#147;<B>Response Notice</B>&#148;) whether it accepts or
rejects the Offer. Failure to deliver a Response Notice within the Acceptance Period will be deemed a rejection of the Offer. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the Response Notice constitutes an acceptance of the Offer, it shall also state the date, place and time on which the sale and purchase of the Sale Shares shall be completed, which shall not be earlier than [ * * * ]
Business Days after the date of the Response Notice. The sale and purchase of the Sale Shares shall take place in accordance with clause 17. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If no Offer is made, or a Response Notice is given (or deemed to be given) which constitutes a rejection of an Offer, the B Shareholder shall not be entitled to transfer its Shares but shall be entitled:
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to serve an IPO Notice under clause 15.6 within [ * * * ] Business Days of the expiry of the Offer Period (if no Offer is made) or the date on which a Response Notice of an Offer is given (or deemed to be given) which
constitutes a rejection; or </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">invoke a further ROFO Process, provided that only one ROFO Notice may be served per Quarter. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.5.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The A Shareholder may, by written notice to the B Shareholder, assign any rights it has under this clause 15.5 to the Company and in this event the Company agrees to be bound by the provisions of this clause 15 as if it
were the A Shareholder. For the avoidance of doubt, any acquisition of Shares by the Company in accordance with this clause 15.5 will not require approval as a Reserved Matter. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>IPO</B><B> Process</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Subject to clause 15.4 and, if applicable, clause 15.6.8(b), the A or B Shareholder (the &#147;<B>Transferring Shareholder</B>&#148;) may by notice in writing (an &#147;<B>IPO Notice</B>&#148;) to the other one (the
&#147;<B>Other Shareholder</B>&#148;) and the Company call for an initial public offering of Shares held by it on a securities exchange (an &#147;<B>IPO</B>&#148;). The IPO Notice shall indicate the number of Shares the Transferring Shareholder
wishes to sell in the IPO subject to the provisions of this clause 15.6. The Board shall determine the applicable exchange taking into account the recommendations of the Valuer and market liquidity and available capital and such other factors as the
Board deems necessary. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt">Within [ * * * ] Business Days of receipt of an IPO Notice, the Company shall engage and instruct an independent
investment bank with expertise in initial public offerings mutually selected by the A and B Shareholders that shall not (unless they agree otherwise) be an underwriter in the competitive process referred to in clause 15.6.4 (the
&#147;<B>Valuer</B>&#148;) to determine and report to the A </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;23&nbsp;- </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
and B Shareholders and the Company within [ * * * ] Business Days of its appointment (the &#147;<B>Report</B>&#148;) on (i)&nbsp;the value of the Company (the &#147;<B>Report Value</B>&#148;);
(ii) an indicative price or price range for the Shares subject to the IPO (the &#147;<B>IPO Value</B>&#148;); (iii) whether the market conditions, business and other relevant factors are conducive and favorable for an IPO; (iv)&nbsp;the most
favorable securities exchange for the IPO; (v)&nbsp;the number of Shares that can be included in the IPO without adversely affecting the price that can be achieved for the Shares through the IPO and (vi)&nbsp;its
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-binding</FONT> recommendation as to what the post IPO capital structure should be and what changes (if any) would need to be made to the rights attaching to the Shares subject to the IPO and/or the Shares to be
retained by the A and B Shareholders post IPO under this Agreement to make the Shares subject to the IPO suitable for listing. It is acknowledged that the aim should be for as many rights to be retained as possible. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Transferring Shareholder shall have [ * * * ] Business Days from delivery of the Report to consider the Report (the &#147;<B>Consideration Period</B>&#148;). If the Transferring Shareholder wishes to pursue an IPO
at a value that equals or exceeds the Report Value or the IPO Value, as the case may be, then it shall notify the Other Shareholder and the Company in writing of the same within the Consideration Period, indicating the number of Shares it wishes to
sell in the IPO (if different from the number included in the IPO Notice) (the &#147;<B>IPO Acceptance Notice</B>&#148;). The Other Shareholder shall respond in writing within [ * * * ] Business Days of receipt of an IPO Acceptance Notice indicating
whether or not it wishes to sell any of its Shares in the IPO subject to any reduction in accordance with clause 15.6.5. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the Transferring Shareholder serves an IPO Acceptance Notice, the Company shall select mutually acceptable underwriter(s) through a competitive process and take all necessary actions to implement the IPO as soon as
practicable and in any event within [ * * * ] months of the date of the IPO Acceptance Notice. The Shareholders shall provide all reasonable assistance in connection with the IPO, including all reasonable assistance to facilitate any due diligence
process, giving such warranties and lock ups and entering into such agreements as are common for an IPO of a comparable size and scope, approving all such matters as may require Shareholder approval and procuring the approval of all such matters as
require Board approval in each case as may be reasonably required to implement the IPO. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Transferring Shareholder (and the Other Shareholder if it delivers a notice under clause 15.6.3) shall be entitled to sell up to such number of the Shares specified in the IPO Acceptance Notice (and, if applicable,
in a notice delivered under clause 15.6.3) in the Company as the lead underwriter confirms can be sold without adversely affecting the price that can be achieved for Shares through the IPO. If any reduction in the number of Shares subject to the IPO
is required, this should be applied: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the Transferring Shareholder is the A Shareholder, pro rata between the A Shares and the B Shares; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;24&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the Transferring Shareholder is the B Shareholder, first against any Shares proposed to be sold by the A Shareholder, so that the B Shareholder will sell the maximum number of IPO Shares possible. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">All expenses incurred by the Company in connection with an IPO shall be paid by the Company. The expenses incurred by a Transferring Shareholder in connection with an IPO shall be for its own account, including the
underwriting commissions payable to underwriters in connection with its sale of Shares pursuant to the IPO. If the Other Shareholder has delivered a notice under clause 15.6.3 and is also selling Shares into the IPO, any such expenses shall be borne
by the selling Shareholders pro rata to the number of Shares each one actually sells in the IPO in accordance with clause 15.6.5. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">In the event that the actual price obtainable by the Transferring Shareholder for the Shares subject to the IPO is less than the Report Value or the IPO Value, as the case may be, the Transferring Shareholder may (in
its sole discretion) by written notice to the Other Shareholder and the Company (a &#147;<B>Termination Notice</B>&#148;) elect to terminate the IPO Process, with respect to such Shares and any Shares of the Other Shareholder if it delivered a
notice under clause 15.6.3, and clause 15.6.8 shall apply. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.6.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If no IPO Acceptance Notice is served or a Termination Notice is served subsequent to an IPO Acceptance Notice, the Transferring Shareholder shall not be entitled to transfer its Shares but shall be entitled:
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the Transferring Shareholder is the A Shareholder, to serve another IPO Notice in accordance with clause 15.6, provided that only one IPO Notice may be served per Quarter; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">if the Transferring Shareholder is the B Shareholder, to invoke a further ROFO Process in accordance with clause 15.5 provided that only one IPO Notice may be served per Quarter. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Transfers after an Initial IPO</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Following an Initial IPO, the provisions of clauses
15.1, 15.2 and 15.4 to 15.6 (inclusive) shall not apply and a Shareholder may sell Shares: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.7.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to a Shareholder Group Entity in accordance with clause 15.3; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.7.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in the market through facilities on which the relevant Shares are listed (and the Company shall, upon request by such Shareholder and at the Company&#146;s cost, take all corporate actions required by applicable Laws,
including the exchange on which the Shares are listed, to facilitate such sale); </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.7.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in accordance with clause 15.8 or 15.9 (if applicable) relating to off market sales; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.7.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in the case of the A Shareholder, to any shareholder of its ultimate parent entity in order to facilitate a sale by such person in accordance with clause 15.7.2; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.7.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in accordance with clause 16 (if applicable) following the occurrence of an Exit Event. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Off market sales by the A Shareholder</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.8.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the A Shareholder proposes to sell Shares representing [ * * * ] or more of the outstanding issued share capital of the Company to a Third Party purchaser (which shall include for these proposes a consortium of
multiple parties) (a &#147;<B>Single Purchaser</B>&#148;) in one or a series of privately negotiated transactions (or in a private or public placement if the A Shareholder is aware that a material portion of the Shares to be sold through such
transaction will be, or is reasonably likely to be, resold to a Single Purchaser) (a &#147;<B>Single Purchaser Sale</B>&#148;), the A Shareholder shall serve a written notice on the B Shareholder including the identity of the potential Single
Purchaser, the number of Shares it proposes to sell, the proposed purchase price for such Shares and such other information reasonably required to enable the B Shareholder to make an informed assessment of whether to participate in the Single
Purchaser Sale (a &#147;<B>Tag Along Notice</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.8.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Within [ * * * ] Business Days of the date of the Tag Along Notice, the B Shareholder must inform the A Shareholder in writing (a &#147;<B>Tag Along Response Notice</B>&#148;) whether it intends to participate in the
Single Purchaser Sale on the terms set out in the Tag Along Notice. If the B Shareholder does not deliver a Tag Along Response Notice within such period, it shall be deemed to have irrevocably declined to participate in the Single Purchaser Sale.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.8.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The B Shareholder shall be entitled to sell in the Single Purchaser Sale the same proportion of its Shares as the proportion of the Shares proposed to be sold by the A Shareholder in the Single Purchaser Sale bears to
the total number of Shares held by the A Shareholder immediately prior to delivery of the Tag Along Notice. If the Single Purchaser is unwilling to purchase all the Shares proposed to be sold following delivery of a Tag Along Response Notice, the
number of Shares to be sold in the Single Purchaser Sale shall be reduced pro rata between the Shares to be sold to the Single Purchaser by the A Shareholder and the Shares to be sold by the B Shareholder. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.8.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If a proposed Single Purchaser Sale has not been completed within [ * * * ] Business Days of receipt of a Tag Along Notice, the A Shareholder shall procure termination of the Single Purchaser Sale. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.8.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">This clause 15.8 will cease to apply once the A Shareholder holds less than [ * * * ] of the Shares. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Off market sales by the B Shareholder</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.9.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the B Shareholder proposes to enter into a Single Purchaser Sale with respect to Shares representing [ * * * ] or more of the outstanding issued share capital of the Company, it shall serve written notice on the A
Shareholder including the identity of the Single Purchaser and the number of Shares it proposes to sell (a &#147;<B>Transfer Notice</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.9.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A Single Purchaser Sale shall not be entered into or completed without the consent of the A Shareholder which must not be unreasonably withheld, taking into account the number of, and rights attaching to, the Shares
proposed to be transferred. Consent shall be deemed to have been given unless, within [ * * * ] Business Days of the date of the Transfer Notice, the A Shareholder serves a written notice of objection on the B Shareholder specifying in reasonable
detail the reasons why it does not consent to the Single Purchase Sale. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.9.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If a proposed Single Purchaser Sale which has received consent (or is deemed to have been consented to) in accordance with clause 15.9.2 has not been completed within 20 Business Days of receipt of a Transfer Notice,
the B Shareholder shall procure termination of the Single Purchaser Sale. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.9.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">This clause 15.9 shall cease to apply once the A Shareholder holds less than [ * * * ] of the Shares or B Shareholder holds less than [ * * * ] of the Shares. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">15.10</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Circumvention of restrictions</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Each Shareholder shall not, and shall procure that its
Affiliates shall not, except as otherwise permitted under this Agreement, employ or be entitled to employ any device or technique or participate in any transaction or arrangements with any person designed to circumvent or avoid the provisions and
restrictions set out in this clause&nbsp;15 or clause 16. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>EXIT EVENTS</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Each party shall promptly inform the Board and the Shareholders as soon as it becomes aware that an Exit Event has occurred. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Defaulting Shareholder is the B Shareholder</B><B> </B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.2.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Except as provided in clause 16.2.2, if the Defaulting Shareholder is the B Shareholder and the Exit Event is not an Insolvency Event, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder shall be
entitled to serve written notice on the Defaulting Shareholder no later than [ * * * ] Business Days after the later of (i)&nbsp;the date on which it becomes aware of the occurrence of an Exit Event and (ii)&nbsp;the relevant date in clause 15.4.3
(if applicable) requiring it to sell all (but not only some) of the Shares held by the Defaulting Shareholder (the &#147;<B>Call Shares</B>&#148;) to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder in cash at the Transfer
Value (such notice, a &#147;<B>Call Notice</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.2.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If the Exit Event is a [ * * * ] </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Defaulting Shareholder is the A Shareholder</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the Defaulting Shareholder is the A
Shareholder and the Exit Event is not an Insolvency Event, the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder shall be entitled to serve written notice on the Defaulting Shareholder no later than [ * * * ] Business Days after the
later of (i)&nbsp;the date on which it becomes aware of the occurrence of an Exit Event and (ii)&nbsp;the relevant date in clause 15.4.3 (if applicable) requiring it to buy all (but not only some) of the Shares held by the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder (the &#147;<B>Put Shares</B>&#148;) in cash at the Transfer Value (such notice, a &#147;<B>Put Notice</B>&#148; and, together with a Call Notice, a &#147;<B>Default Notice</B>&#148;). </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;27&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
