<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Exit Event is an Insolvency Event</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">If the Exit Event is an Insolvency Event, the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder shall be entitled to serve a Call Notice on the Defaulting Shareholder no later than [ * * * ] Business Days after becoming aware of the occurrence of such Insolvency Event. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Terms of Default Notice</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.5.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">A transfer of Shares pursuant to a Default Notice shall be subject to the following terms: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the Default Notice shall be irrevocable and unconditional; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">unless clause 16.6 applies, completion of the sale and purchase of the Call Shares or Put Shares (as the case may be) shall take place on the later of: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="23%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(i)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the [ * * * ] Business Day following the expiry of a period of [ * * * ] Business Days from the date of the Default Notice if the relevant Exit Event is a Terminating Breach which is capable of remedy but has not been
remedied in full (at the Defaulting Shareholder&#146;s cost) to the satisfaction of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="23%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(ii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the [ * * * ] Business Day following the date of the Default Notice with respect to any other Exit Event; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="23%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(iii)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the [ * * * ] Business Day following the date on which the Transfer Value is agreed or determined, </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">(the &#147;<B>Transfer Date</B>&#148;) and otherwise in accordance with clause 17. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.5.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">For the avoidance of doubt: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">only the B Shareholder is entitled to serve a Default Notice following a Acorn/JAB Change of Control Event, a Competitor Event, an Insolvency Event relating to the A Shareholder or an event described in paragraphs
(b)&nbsp;and (c) of the definition of Terminating Breach or paragraph (a)&nbsp;to the extent of a breach by the A Shareholder; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">only the A Shareholder is entitled to serve a Default Notice following a MDLZ Change of Control Event, an Insolvency Event relating to the B Shareholder or paragraph (a)&nbsp;of the definition of Terminating Breach to
the extent of a breach by the B Shareholder. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Completion of transfers</B><B><I> </I></B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.6.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The purchasing Shareholder will use its best endeavours to secure financing on commercially reasonable terms and conditions to enable completion of the sale and purchase of the Call Shares or Put Shares (as the case may
be) by the Transfer Date. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL
TREATMENT HAS BEEN REQUESTED FOR PORTIONS OF THIS EXHIBIT. THE COPY FILED HEREWITH OMITS THE INFORMATION SUBJECT TO A CONFIDENTIALITY REQUEST. OMISSIONS ARE DESIGNATED [&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;]. A COMPLETE VERSION OF THIS EXHIBIT HAS BEEN FILED
SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;28&nbsp;- </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.6.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If, notwithstanding its best endeavours, the purchasing Shareholder is not able to fund the Transfer Value by the Transfer Date, it shall be entitled to serve a notice (a &#147;<B>Deferral Notice</B>&#148;) on the
selling Shareholder deferring completion of the sale and purchase of the Call Shares or Put Shares (as the case may be) to a date which is as soon as possible after the Transfer Date but in any event not later than [ * * * ] months after the date of
the Default Notice (the &#147;<B>Longstop Date</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.6.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The A Shareholder may, by written notice to the B Shareholder, assign any rights it has under clauses 16.2 and 16.4 to the Company and in this event the Company agrees to be bound by the provisions of this clause 16 as
if it were the A Shareholder. For the avoidance of doubt, any acquisition of Shares by the Company in accordance with this clause 16 will not require approval as a Reserved Matter. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Exit Event</B><B>s</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the purposes of this clause 16 an &#147;<B>Exit Event</B>&#148;
shall be deemed to have occurred when: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">a Terminating Breach has occurred which, if capable of remedy, has not been remedied within [ * * * ] Business Days of the Defaulting Shareholder being served with written notice identifying the breach and requiring it
to be remedied; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">at any time prior to an Initial IPO, Oak or Oak Minority ceases to be Controlled by Acorn Holdings B.V. and/or Acorn Holdings B.V. ceases to be Controlled by JAB Holdings B.V. other than as the result of a bona fide
reorganisation of its business/a merger into any successor entity as part of a merger transaction or equivalent pursuant to which all or substantially all of the persons who are beneficial owners of the outstanding securities immediately prior to
such transaction beneficially own, directly or indirectly, more than 50% of the outstanding securities of the entity resulting from such transaction in substantially the same proportions (a &#147;<B>Acorn/JAB</B> <B>Change of Control</B>&#148;);
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">at any time prior to an Initial IPO, [ * * * ]; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">at any time prior to an Initial IPO (i)&nbsp;a Restricted Person described in paragraph (b)&nbsp;of the definition acquires any shares in Acorn Holdings B.V. except to the extent of shares acquired by investors in a
shareholder of Acorn Holdings B.V. which is a limited partnership on a distribution of shares in Acorn Holdings B.V. in accordance with terms of such partnership&#146;s governing documents or (ii)&nbsp;a Restricted Person described in paragraphs
(a)&nbsp;or (b) of the definition acquires any shares from Acorn Holdings B.V. or JAB Holdings B.V. or any of its Affiliates (a &#147;<B>Competitor Event</B>&#148;); </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the A Shareholder or B Shareholder is subject to an Insolvency Event; or </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">16.7.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">after the third anniversary of Closing, the B Shareholder withholds its approval to the Reserved Matter set out in paragraph 19 of schedule 1 for two consecutive Financial Years and the Escalation Representatives fail
to resolve the issue as a Deadlock Matter within the Deadlock Resolution Period, </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">the A or B Shareholder in respect of which
an Exit Event has occurred shall be a &#147;<B>Defaulting Shareholder</B>&#148; and the other one shall be the &#147;<B><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">Non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder</B>&#148;. </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>COMPLETION OF SHARE TRANSFERS</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Transfer terms</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Shares shall be transferred free of all Encumbrances and together with all rights attaching thereto as at the date of the relevant transfer. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Prior to an Initial IPO, a Shareholder must transfer all (but not only some) of its Shares (unless clause 15.6 applies) and must transfer both the legal and beneficial ownership of the relevant Shares.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.1.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">All Shareholder Instruments held by such Shareholder must be transferred at the same time and to the same transferee as the Shares. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Completion of transfer</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Except in connection with or following an Initial IPO, the
completion of any transfer of Shares under this Agreement shall be made in accordance with the following terms: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the purchaser shall not be a Restricted Person; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the seller shall deliver to the purchaser a draft notarial deed of transfer to be promptly and duly executed before a Dutch <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">civil-law</FONT> notary in favour of the purchaser and a
certified copy of any authority under which such transfer will be executed; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the purchaser shall cooperate with respect to such deed of transfer; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the purchaser shall pay the aggregate transfer price in respect of the relevant Shares to the seller by banker&#146;s draft for value on the date of completion or in such other manner as the purchaser and the seller may
agree prior to completion; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the purchaser shall (if it is not already a party to this Agreement) enter into a Deed of Adherence substantially in the form set out in schedule 8; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.2.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the seller shall do all such other acts and execute all such other documents in a form satisfactory to the purchaser as the purchaser may reasonably require to give effect to the transfer of Shares to it.
</TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Failure to transfer</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If clause 16.2 or clause 16.4 applies and the Defaulting Shareholder fails to comply with its obligations to transfer Call Shares in accordance with clause 16.5.1(b), the Company shall authorise a person to execute and
deliver the necessary transfer on its behalf. The Company shall receive the purchase money in respect of such transfer in trust for that Shareholder (and the Company shall not be required to account to such Shareholder for any interest accrued on
such amount) and the receipt of the Company for the purchase money shall be a good discharge for the purchaser, who shall not be bound to see the application of the purchase money. The Company shall, subject to the instrument of transfer being duly
executed, cause the purchaser to be registered as holder of the relevant Shares. Once registration has taken place in purported exercise of the power contained in this clause 17.3 the validity of the proceedings shall not be questioned by any
person. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If clause 15.5.4 or clause 16.5.1(b) (in so far as it relates to a sale and purchase of Put Shares) applies and a Shareholder fails to comply with its obligations to transfer Shares in accordance with those clauses:
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the Defaulting Shareholder shall be deemed to have waived its right to exercise any of its powers or rights in relation to the management of, and participation in the profits of, the Company under this Agreement, the
Articles or otherwise; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the provisions of clauses 15, 17.1 and 17.2.1 shall cease to apply to the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder with respect to the Shares held by it and the
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-defaulting</FONT> Shareholder shall be free to transfer its Shares to a Third Party without restriction. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Validity of Share transfers </B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A transfer of a Share to any person shall only be valid if
the transfer has been carried out in accordance with this Agreement and the Articles and in no other circumstances. Any purported transfer of Shares made other than as provided for in this Agreement shall be void. Unless the Shareholders determine
otherwise prior to an IPO, Shares can only be held by persons that have become a party to this Agreement by executing a Deed of Adherence in accordance with clause 17.2.5. The Shareholders undertake that they shall consent to the execution of Deed
of Adherence by any proposed transferee of Shares to whom the transfer of such Shares is allowed in accordance with the terms of this Agreement. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">17.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Step down of rights following B Shareholder transfer</B><B> </B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">With effect from the date
on which, solely as a result of transfer(s) by the B Shareholder, the B shareholder holds less than [ * * * ] of the Shares, this Agreement shall be amended as set out in schedule 13 (the &#147;<B>Step Down</B>&#148;); provided that a transfer of B
Shares to (a)&nbsp;any Affiliate of the B Shareholder and (b)&nbsp;the A Shareholder or one of its Affiliates, in each case in connection with the closing of the acquisition of Maple, shall not be considered a transfer for purposes of this clause
17.5 and no Step Down shall occur solely as a result of such transfer. Save as amended by schedule 13, this Agreement shall remain in full force and effect unless and until terminated in accordance with clause&nbsp;20. </P>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">18.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>REGULATORY CONSENTS FOR TRANSFERS</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">18.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If a transfer of Shares is permitted by, or required to be effected under, this Agreement but requires or is likely to require a Regulatory Consent, the Shareholders and the Company: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">18.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">agree that the completion of such transfer shall be conditional upon such Regulatory Consent being obtained; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">18.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">agree that any procedure or time period to be followed under this Agreement to effect the transfer shall, subject to clause 18.2, be extended until such time as the relevant Regulatory Consent has been obtained;
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">18.1.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">shall at the purchaser&#146;s cost use reasonable endeavours to assist the purchaser in obtaining such Regulatory Consent including, but not limited to: </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">providing and/or procuring that the Company and each relevant Group Company provide all information necessary and reasonably within their control which the purchaser may reasonably request, to enable the purchaser to
determine which Regulatory Consents are required in connection with the transfer or the issue; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">ensuring that all such information necessary and reasonably within their control which the purchaser may reasonably request for making (or responding to any requests for further information following) any notification,
submission, communication or filing in connection with the seeking of the Regulatory Consent is available to the person required to obtain the Regulatory Consent or who is dealing with the notification, submission, communication or filing, and is
accurately and promptly provided upon request, </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:15%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">provided that any commercially sensitive information may be provided on a
counsel to counsel basis or directly to the relevant authority. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">18.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">If any Regulatory Consent has not been obtained within [ * * * ] months of the application being made (the &#147;<B>Regulatory</B> <B>Longstop Date</B>&#148;), the relevant purchaser shall not be entitled to acquire the
Shares unless, immediately before the expiry of the [ * * * ] month period, Regulatory Consent has not been obtained but is still in process, in which case the Regulatory Longstop Date shall be deemed to be extended until the earlier of (i)&nbsp;the
date on which Regulatory Consent is obtained or (ii)&nbsp;the date on which Regulatory Consent becomes incapable of being obtained, provided that the process continues to be diligently pursued. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

obtained the necessary consent in accordance with clause 6, the Company shall not allot the New Shares other than in accordance with this clause 19, provided that the provisions of the clause 19.3 shall not apply (i)&nbsp;to the issue of Management
</P></TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">
Equity or (ii)&nbsp;the issue of New Shares in connection with any mergers or acquisitions or joint venture transactions in either case save where, following the issue of such New Shares, an A or
B Shareholder&#146;s aggregate holding of Shares would be reduced to below [ * * * ] of the outstanding issued share capital of the Company in which case the provisions of clause 19.3 shall apply with respect to that Shareholder. </TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Company shall issue a notice to the Shareholders confirming its intention to issue New Shares and shall make an offer to each Shareholder to allot to it a proportion of the New Shares as nearly as practicable equal
to the proportion in nominal value of the Shares held by it as at close of business on the date before such offers (&#147;<B>Relevant Proportion</B>&#148;). Shareholders may take up all or part or none of the New Shares offered to them.
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">23.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">No announcement, communication or circular in connection with the existence or the subject matter of this Agreement shall be made or issued by or on behalf of any Shareholder or any of its Affiliates without the prior
written approval of the A and B Shareholders or the A or B Shareholder if the Shareholder making the announcement is an A or B Shareholder (such approval not to be unreasonably withheld or delayed). </TD></TR></TABLE>

prepared on the basis that there would be a single A Shareholder (Oak) and a single B Shareholder (MDLZ). However, Oak Minority (as well as Oak) now holds A Shares. The parties therefore agree that, in this Agreement (unless expressly provided
otherwise), Oak and Oak Minority shall together be treated as a single A Shareholder for all purposes and that this Agreement shall be construed accordingly. In particular: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">28.9.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">any notice to be sent to the A Shareholder or Oak or Oak Minority may be addressed to either Oak or Oak Minority (or both of them); </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;39&nbsp;- </P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">28.9.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">any consent to be given by the A Shareholder or Oak or Oak Minority may be signed by either Oak or Oak Minority (or both of them) and a signature by one will be sufficient; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">28.9.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">a breach of this Agreement by either Oak or Oak Minority shall be treated as a breach by both of them, and Oak and Oak Minority shall be jointly and severally liable for any liability of either of them arising out of or
in connection with this Agreement. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The parties agree that the introduction of a second holder of A Shares shall not increase
the liabilities of the B Shareholder or any of its Affiliates (compared to the position if all the A Shares were held by a single person). </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">29.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>ASSIGNMENT</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">29.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">This Agreement shall be binding on and enure for the benefit of each party&#146;s successors in title. Save in connection with a transfer made to a Shareholder Group Entity in accordance with clause 15.3 (or as provided
in clause 29.2) no party shall, without the prior written consent of the other parties, assign, transfer, grant any security interest over or create any trust in respect of, or purport to assign, transfer, grant any security interest over or create
any trust in respect of, any of its rights or obligations under this Agreement. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">29.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">MDLZ may, prior to Closing and without further consent of the other parties, give notice of its intention to novate this Agreement to another Shareholder Group Entity (the &#147;<B>MDLZ Shareholder</B>&#148;). Following
receipt of a notice to this effect, the parties shall enter into a novation agreement in accordance with which: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">29.2.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the MDLZ Shareholder shall perform MDLZ&#146;s obligations under this Agreement and be bound by the terms of this Agreement in every way as if the MDLZ Shareholder had at all times been a party to this Agreement in
place of MDLZ and references to &#147;MDLZ&#148; in this Agreement shall be references to the MDLZ Shareholder; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">29.2.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">save as in relation to continuing obligations of confidentiality in relation to confidential information received pursuant to this Agreement, the other parties shall release and discharge MDLZ from further performance
of this Agreement and all liabilities, claims and demands howsoever arising under this Agreement, whether in contract, tort or otherwise, and accept the liability of the MDLZ Shareholder under this Agreement in place of the liability of MDLZ; and
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">29.2.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the other parties shall perform their respective obligations under this Agreement and be bound by the terms of this Agreement in every way as if the MDLZ Shareholder had at all times been a party to this Agreement in
place of MDLZ. </TD></TR></TABLE>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">31.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>GOVERNING LAW</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:7%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">This Agreement and any
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-contractual</FONT> or other obligations arising out of or in connection with it are governed by Dutch law. </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">32.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>ARBITRATION</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">32.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Any dispute, controversy or claim arising from or connected with this Agreement, including one regarding the existence, validity or termination of this Agreement or the consequences of its nullity or relating to any <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-contractual</FONT> or other dispute arising from or connected with this Agreement shall be referred to and finally resolved by arbitration under the rules of the London Court of International Arbitration (the
&#147;<B>LCIA</B> <B>Rules</B>&#148;). </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">32.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The arbitral tribunal shall consist of three arbitrators. The claimant(s) shall nominate one arbitrator and the respondent(s) shall nominate one arbitrator, and the two arbitrators thus nominated, once appointed by the
London Court of International Arbitration (the &#147;<B>LCIA Court</B>&#148;), shall nominate a third arbitrator as chairman of the arbitral tribunal within fifteen days of the last of their appointments. In the event that the claimant(s) or the
respondent(s) fail(s) to nominate an arbitrator within the time limits specified by the LCIA Rules, or the party nominated arbitrators fail to agree the chairman of the arbitral tribunal within the time limits specified in the preceding sentence,
such arbitrator shall be appointed promptly by the LCIA Court. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">32.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The seat of the arbitration shall be London, England, all hearings shall take place in London, England, and the language of the arbitration shall be English. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">32.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Each party waives any right to refer points of law or to appeal to the courts, to the extent that such waiver can validly be made. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">32.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The parties agree that the arbitral tribunal shall have the power to order on a provisional basis any relief which it would have power to grant in a final award. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>COMMITTEES </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>PART A:
AUDIT COMMITTEE TERMS OF REFERENCE </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Composition and Meetings of the Audit Committee</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The Audit Committee comprises not less than two Directors, including at least one A Director and at least one B Director. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The initial composition of the Audit Committee shall be Bart Becht, Byron Trott, Olivier Goudet, Alejandro Santo Domingo and up to 3 members identified by MDLZ prior to Closing. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The chairman of the Audit Committee shall be appointed by the B Shareholder. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The chairman will ensure that the Committee receives information and papers in a timely manner to enable full and proper consideration to be given to the issues. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The quorum for meetings of the Audit Committee is two of its members which must include one A Director and one B Director. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">No one other than an Audit Committee member is entitled to attend meetings of the Audit Committee but others may attend by invitation. The Audit Committee may invite any officer, director, employee of or adviser to the
Group to attend for all or part of any meeting as and when appropriate and necessary. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">The external auditor and CFO will be invited to attend meetings of the Audit Committee on a regular basis. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">Meetings of the Audit Committee are to be held at least four times in each Financial Year at appropriate times in the financial reporting and audit cycle and otherwise as required. Any of the Committee members, the CFO,
head of internal audit (if appointed) or the Company&#146;s external auditors may request a meeting of the Audit Committee if he considers it necessary. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">1.9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">At least 10 Business Days&#146; written notice of an Audit Committee meeting shall be given to each member of the Audit Committee and any other person required to attend. Supporting papers shall be sent to the Audit
Committee members and to other attendees as appropriate, at the same time. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Authorisations</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Audit Committee is authorised by the Board to: </P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">investigate any activity within its terms of reference; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">obtain any information it requires from any employee of a Group Company and to call any employee to be questioned at a meeting of the Audit Committee as and when required (and all employees are directed to <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">co-operate</FONT> with any request made by the Audit Committee); </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL
TREATMENT HAS BEEN REQUESTED FOR PORTIONS OF THIS EXHIBIT. THE COPY FILED HEREWITH OMITS THE INFORMATION SUBJECT TO A CONFIDENTIALITY REQUEST. OMISSIONS ARE DESIGNATED [&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;]. A COMPLETE VERSION OF THIS EXHIBIT HAS BEEN FILED
SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;50&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">make recommendations to the Board; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">obtain, at the Company&#146;s expense, such independent, legal, accounting or other professional advice on any matter it deems reasonably necessary; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">2.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">secure the attendance of other persons at its meetings if it considers this necessary. </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"><B>Duties of the Audit Committee</B> </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The duties of the Audit Committee are: </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>External audit </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">in respect of the external audit: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to consider and make recommendations to the Board in relation to the appointment, reappointment and removal of the external auditors. If an auditor resigns, the Audit Committee shall investigate the issues leading to
this and decide whether any action is required; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to oversee the selection process for new auditors and ensure that all tendering firms have such access as is necessary to information and individuals during the duration of the tendering process; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to consider and approve the remuneration of the external auditors, including fees for both audit and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services and that the level of fees are appropriate to enable an
effective and high quality audit to be conducted; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to approve the terms of engagement of the external auditors, including the engagement letter issued at the start of each audit and the scope of the audit and to discuss with the external auditors before the audit starts
the nature and scope of the audit. The scope shall include a review of all transactions between a Group Company and a Shareholder or any of its Affiliates or the Shareholders of Acorn Holdings B.V. from time to time or their Affiliates;
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to meet regularly with the external auditors, including once at the planning stage before the audit and once after the audit at the reporting stage. The Audit Committee shall meet the external auditors at least once in
each Financial Year, without management being present, to discuss its remit and any issues arising from the audit; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to review the findings of the audit with the external auditors. This shall include, but not be limited to, the following: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">a discussion of any major issues which arose during the audit; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">key accounting and audit judgements; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(c)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">level of errors identified during the audit; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(d)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the effectiveness of the audit process. </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL
TREATMENT HAS BEEN REQUESTED FOR PORTIONS OF THIS EXHIBIT. THE COPY FILED HEREWITH OMITS THE INFORMATION SUBJECT TO A CONFIDENTIALITY REQUEST. OMISSIONS ARE DESIGNATED [&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;*&nbsp;]. A COMPLETE VERSION OF THIS EXHIBIT HAS BEEN FILED
SEPARATELY WITH THE SECURITIES AND EXCHANGE COMMISSION. </P>

 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">-&nbsp;51&nbsp;- </P>


<p Style='page-break-before:always'>
<HR  SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.7</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to keep under review the scope and results of the audit, the audit fee and its cost effectiveness, taking into consideration relevant professional and regulatory requirements; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.8</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to review: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(a)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">any representation letters requested by the external auditors before they are signed by management; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="15%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">(b)</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the external auditor&#146;s management letter and response to the auditor&#146;s findings and recommendations; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.9</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to develop and implement a policy on the supply of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services by the external auditors to avoid any threat to auditor objectivity and independence, taking into account any
relevant ethical guidance on the matter, and to keep such policy under review; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.10</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to assess annually the external auditor&#146;s independence and objectivity taking into account relevant professional and regulatory requirements and the relationship with the external auditors as a whole, including the
provision of any <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-audit</FONT> services; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.11</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to satisfy itself that there are no relationships (such as family, employment, investment, financial or business) between the external auditors and the Group (other than in the ordinary course of business) which could
adversely affect the auditor&#146;s independence and objectivity; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.12</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to monitor the external auditor&#146;s compliance with relevant ethical and professional guidance on the rotation of external audit partners, the level of fees paid by the Company compared to the overall fee income of
the firm, office and partner and other related requirements; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.13</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to assess annually the qualifications, expertise and resources of the external auditors and the effectiveness of the audit process which shall include a report from the external auditors on their own internal quality
procedures; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.14</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to evaluate the risks to the quality and effectiveness of the financial reporting process and to consider the need to include the risk of the withdrawal of their auditor from the market in that evaluation; and
</TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.1.15</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to discuss problems and reservations arising from audits and any matters the auditors may wish to discuss (in the absence of executive directors, where necessary); </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Financial statements </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to review and monitor the integrity of the financial statements of the Company and the Group including the annual accounts and any other formal document or announcements relating to financial performance, reviewing
significant financial reporting issues and judgements which they contain; </TD></TR></TABLE>
 <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">CONFIDENTIAL

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the Audit Committee shall review and challenge where necessary: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the consistency of, and any changes to, significant accounting policies both on a <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-on-year</FONT></FONT> basis and across the Company and/or the
Group; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the methods used to account for significant or unusual transactions where different approaches are possible; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">whether the Company and/or the Group has followed appropriate accounting standards and made appropriate estimates and judgements, taking into account the views of the external auditors; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">the clarity and completeness of disclosure in the Company&#146;s and other members of the Group&#146;s financial reports and the context in which statements are made; and </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.3.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">where the Audit Committee is not satisfied with any aspect of the proposed financial reporting by the Company, to report its views to the Board. </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to submit the documents referred to in paragraph 3.3 to the Board for its approval and to determine what information should be brought to the Board&#146;s attention in connection with that submission; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Internal controls and risk management systems </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to keep under review the adequacy and effectiveness of the Group&#146;s internal financial controls and internal control and risk management systems; </TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Internal audit </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">where an internal audit function exists: </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.1</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">review and approve the remit of the internal audit function and ensure the function has the necessary resources and access to information to enable it to fulfil its mandate, and is equipped to perform in accordance with
appropriate professional standards for internal auditors; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.2</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to consider and make recommendations to the Board regarding the appointment and removal of the head of the internal audit function; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to review and assess the annual internal audit plan; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.4</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">receive a report on the results of the internal auditor&#146;s work on a periodic basis; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="8%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">3.6.5</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to review and monitor management&#146;s responsiveness to the findings and recommendations of the internal auditor; </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%">&nbsp;</TD>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">to meet the head of internal audit at least once in each Financial Year, without management being present, to discuss their remit and any issues arising from the internal audit reviews carried out and give the head of
the internal audit function a right of direct access to the Audit Committee; and </TD></TR></TABLE>

<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD WIDTH="7%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">4.3</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top">oversee any investigation of activities which are within its terms of reference; and </TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
